1\n\t}\n\n\treturn Stats{\n\t\tCount:   count,\n\t\tAverage: average,\n\t\tP99:     durations[p99Index],\n\t}\n}\n\n// Reset clears all recorded durations.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) Reset() {\n\tdt.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.Unlock()\n\tdt.durations = make([]time.Duration, 0)\n}\n```\n\n### 2. The solution tracks wall-clock duration of each evaluation, provides aggregate statistics (count, average, P99), and is thread-safe for concurrent use.\n\n## Implementation Status\n\nI've encountered a filesystem permissions issue where the `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/` directory is owned by root with restricted permissions. The changes below need to be applied manually or by a user with appropriate permissions.\n\n##  Files to Create/Modify\n\n### 1. CREATE: internal/server/evaluation/duration_tracker.go\n\n```go\npackage evaluation\n\nimport (\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"sync\"\n\t\"time\"\n)\n\n// DurationTracker tracks evaluation latencies and provides aggregate statistics.\n// It is safe for concurrent use.\ntype DurationTracker struct {\n\tmu        sync.RWMutex\n\tdurations []time.Duration\n}\n\n// Stats represents aggregate duration statistics.\ntype Stats struct {\n\t// Count is the total number of recorded evaluations.\n\tCount int64\n\t// Average is the mean duration of all evaluations in nanoseconds.\n\tAverage time.Duration\n\t// P99 is the 99th percentile duration in nanoseconds.\n\tP99 time.Duration\n}\n\n// NewDurationTracker creates a new DurationTracker.\nfunc NewDurationTracker() *DurationTracker {\n\treturn &DurationTracker{\n\t\tdurations: make([]time.Duration, 0),\n\t}\n}\n\n// Record records a duration for an evaluation.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) Record(d time.Duration) {\n\tdt.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.Unlock()\n\tdt.durations = append(dt.durations, d)\n}\n\n// GetStats returns aggregate statistics about recorded evaluations.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) GetStats() Stats {\n\tdt.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tcount := int64(len(dt.durations))\n\tif count == 0 {\n\t\treturn Stats{Count: 0}\n\t}\n\n\t// Calculate average\n\tvar total time.Duration\n\tfor _, d := range dt.durations {\n\t\ttotal += d\n\t}\n\taverage := total / time.Duration(count)\n\n\t// Calculate P99 by sorting\n\t// Create a copy to avoid modifying the original slice\n\tdurations := make([]time.Duration, len(dt.durations))\n\tcopy(durations, dt.durations)\n\tsort.Slice(durations, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\treturn durations[i] < durations[j]\n\t})\n\n\t// Calculate 99th percentile index\n\tp99Index := int(float64(count-1) * 0.99)\n\tif p99Index >= len(durations) {\n\t\tp99Index = len(durations) - 1\n\t}\n\n\treturn Stats{\n\t\tCount:   count,\n\t\tAverage: average,\n\t\tP99:     durations[p99Index],\n\t}\n}\n\n// Reset clears all recorded durations.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) Reset() {\n\tdt.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.Unlock()\n\tdt.durations = make([]time.Duration, 0)\n}\n```\n\n### 2. The solution tracks wall-clock duration of each evaluation, provides aggregate statistics (count, average, P99), and is thread-safe for concurrent use.\n\n## Implementation Status\n\nI've encountered a filesystem permissions issue where the `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/` directory is owned by root with restricted permissions. 1\n\t}\n\n\treturn Stats{\n\t\tCount:   count,\n\t\tAverage: average,\n\t\tP99:     durations[p99Index],\n\t}\n}\n\n// Reset clears all recorded durations.\nfunc (dt *DurationTracker) Reset() {\n\tdt.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer dt.mu.Unlock()\n\tdt.durations = make([]time.Duration, 0)\n}\n```\n\n### 2.
